\newcommand{\storybox}[3]{% #1=x, #2=y, #3=text
  \begin{textblock}{3}(#1,#2)
    \noindent%
    \begin{tikzpicture}
      \node[rectangle, rounded corners=3pt, fill=white, inner sep=0.1in, text width=2.55in, align=left] {%
        \small\sffamily #3%
      };
    \end{tikzpicture}%
  \end{textblock}%
}

{\Huge\sffamily\bfseries No Time to Discourse}

{\Large\sffamily A Speculative Atlas of Climate Disaster}

\vspace{0.5in}

{\large\sffamily A Procedurally Generated Novel}

\vspace{1in}

{\large\sffamily by Mark Sample}

\vfill

{\normalsize\sffamily Generated November 24, 2025}

\end{titlepage}

% About page
\newpage
\section*{About This Novel}

\noindent\textit{No Time to Discourse} is a speculative atlas that explores climate disaster across North America through interactive mapping and generative flash fiction.

\vspace{0.3in}

\noindent This novel was generated for NaNoGenMo (National Novel Generation Month), transforming the web-based interactive experience of https://notime.now/ into a print format. Each page combines watercolor maps from Stamen Design with works of flash fiction, which are procedurally-generated through bespoke RiTa.js grammars developed by Mark Sample.

\vspace{0.3in}

\noindent Each of the stories in this novel is a work of fiction, yet each also attempts to capture at a human level the realities of climate disaster.

\vspace{0.3in}

\noindent\textbf{Original Web Project:} \url{https://notime.now/}

\noindent\textbf{Code Repository:} \url{https://github.com/samplereality/no-time-to-discourse-novel}

\clearpage

% Henry V quote on its own page
\vspace*{\fill}
\begin{center}
  {\Large\textit{"The day is hot, and the weather, and the wars, and the King,\\
  and the Dukes; it is no time to discourse."}}

  \vspace{0.3in}

  --- Henry V
\end{center}

\storybox{3.33}{7.97}{\textbf{Swift Current, Saskatchewan}\\[0.1in]
\textit{Wednesday, April 7, 2027}\\
 Riley boils her water before drinking. The storm didn't even have a name, she thinks. Angela saw the flash flooding wash away trees, cars, houses. Nightjar Diner Co.. The flooding in Swift Current didn't even make the national news. }

\storybox{5.19}{4.74}{\textbf{Moose Jaw, Saskatchewan}\\[0.1in]
\textit{Sunday, January 28, 2029}\\
 ``It's a scorcher today,'' they say. Today? You mean this year. The road to Pla-Mor Palace is jammed with abandoned cars, shimmering in the heat. The ambient sound of ten thousand HVACs washes over the land.}

\storybox{1.61}{4.17}{\textbf{Regina, Saskatchewan}\\[0.1in]
\textit{Monday, June 4, 2029}\\
 There's too much water, thinks Cyrus. He didn't think it would be this bad. Gunky dark water sloshes around Aryan's parlor. A used plastic bag bobs in the  water. The flooding in Regina didn't even make the national news. }

You couldn't see, especially if you didn't wanna see. But 2090, that was the year.''}

Now he regretted everything as the roof began to leak. Three feet of mud covered everything he ever owned. He wondered if this was God's way of saying the coast was no longer for sale.}
